Usage: java -jar n4jsc.jar [options] FILE FILE ...
 FILE                                                            : filename of source (or project, see -bt) to compile
 --buildType (-bt) [singlefile | projects | allprojects |        : provide the type to build (defaults to dontcompile). 
 dontcompile]                                                      'allprojects' compiles all projects found in the
                                                                   projectlocations, no other argument required.
                                                                   'projects' interprets the arguments as projects-folders and
                                                                   compiles them.
                                                                   'singlefile' interprets the arguments as paths to N4JS-source
                                                                   files and compiles only those both.
                                                                   'dontcompile' don't generate anything. (default: dontcompile)
 --clean (-c)                                                    : use this flag to indicate that the output folder should be
                                                                   cleaned before compilation. If this flag is activated, the
                                                                   flag -bt must be activated as well. This flag can NOT be used
                                                                   in combination with -bt singlefile. (default: false)
 --debug                                                         : print information about the current setup of the compiler
                                                                   (default: true)
 --help (-h)                                                     : print help & exit (default: true)
 --implementationId (-impl) ID                                   : if there are API projects among the dependencies of the module
                                                                   to run, this specifies the ID of the implementation to use;
                                                                   only required when running/testing if there are API projects
                                                                   and there exists more than one implementation.
 --installMissingDependencies (-imd)                             : usually projects have dependencies that have to be fetched
                                                                   before the compilation. If this flag is provided, compiler
                                                                   will calculate missing dependencies based on the manifest
                                                                   files of the projects provided as input to the
                                                                   compilation.Calculated missing dependencies will be fetched by
                                                                   Library Manager priori to the compilation. (default: false)
 --keepCompiling                                                 : keep compiling - even if errors are encountered (default:
                                                                   false)
 --listRunners (-lr)                                             : show list of available runners. (default: false)
 --listTesters (-lt)                                             : show list of available testers (default: false)
 --nodejsLocation FILE                                           : when configured then the Node.js binary located under the
                                                                   given absolute path will be used for executing modules. When
                                                                   specified then the absolute path of the folder that contains
                                                                   the Node.js binary should be specified. If not set, then the
                                                                   default /usr/local/bin (on Unix systems) or C:\Program
                                                                   Files\nodejs (on Windows systems) location will be used to
                                                                   look for the Node.js binary.
 --notests                                                       : don't process test-folders (default: false)
 --npmrcRootLocation FILE                                        : when configured then the nprc setting used from given pathwill
                                                                   be used for installing npm packages modules. When specified
                                                                   then the absolute path of the folder that contains the
                                                                   '.npmrc' file should be specified. If not set, then the
                                                                   default to value specified by 'user.home' property value
                                                                   returned by java.lang.System
 --preferences FILE                                              : provide custom compiler preference settings stored in a
                                                                   *.properties file
 --projectlocations (-pl) directory                              : provide folder(s) to search for projects. If not set, the base
                                                                   folder of the running jvm will be taken as the location.
                                                                   Multiple folders can be given separated by the systems
                                                                   path-separator(: or ;). Only direct subfolders will be queried
                                                                   for projects.
 --run (-r) pathToFileToRun                                      : path to the file that should be run after compilation.
 --runWith (-rw) runnerId                                        : ID of runner to use, last segment is sufficient, e.g. nodejs.
                                                                   (default: nodejs)
 --systemLoader (-sl) VAL                                        : when specified the given javascript system loader will be used
                                                                   for running the module. If not specified, the by default the
                                                                   System.js loader will be used. The following system loaders
                                                                   are available: sjs and cjs where sjs stands for System.js and
                                                                   cjs stands for Common JS.
 --targetPlatformInstallLocation (-tl) FILE                      : if specified and the target platform file is given as well,
                                                                   then all third party dependencies specified in the target
                                                                   platform file will be downloaded to that given location. If
                                                                   the target platform file is given, but the target platform
                                                                   install location is not specified, then a the compilation
                                                                   phase will be aborted and the execution will be interrupted.If
                                                                   --targetPlatformSkipInstall is provided this parameter is
                                                                   ignored.
 --test (-t) path                                                : path must point to a project, folder, or file containing tests.
 --testCatalogFile (-tc) FILE                                    : if specified, a test catalog file will be generated to the
                                                                   given file location. The generated test catalog file will
                                                                   represent all tests that are available among the compiled
                                                                   sources. If the file does not exists at the given location, a
                                                                   new file will be created to the specified location. If a file
                                                                   already exists at the given location then the content of the
                                                                   existing file content will be replaced with the newly
                                                                   assembled test catalog. If an invalid file location is
                                                                   specified as the test catalog file output, then the catalog
                                                                   generation will fail.
 --testReportRoot FILE                                           : when provided, it is expected to be directory in which test
                                                                   report will be written.If test report already exists in that
                                                                   location it is removed overwritten. If not provided, test
                                                                   report generation is skipped.
